    Title = "Auto Hop Elite",
    Description = "Hop server if Elite Hunter is on cooldown",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        _G.HopElite = Value
    end
})

-- ==========================================
-- LOGIC: HOP SERVER (DÙNG CHUNG)
-- ==========================================
local function HopServer()
    local RF = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):WaitForChild("__ServerBrowser")
    local best = { Bounty = 0, JobId = nil }

    for i = 1, 100 do
        local ok, res = pcall(RF.InvokeServer, RF, i)
        if ok and typeof(res) == "table" then
            for jobId, data in pairs(res) do
                local bounty = tonumber(data.Bounty) or 0
                local players = data.Count or data.Players or 0
                if bounty > best.Bounty and players < 12 then
                    best.JobId = jobId
                    best.Bounty = bounty
                    best.Players = players
                end
            end
        end
        task.wait()
    end

    if best.JobId then
        RF:InvokeServer("teleport", best.JobId)
    else
        local HttpService = game:GetService("HttpService")
        local TPService = game:GetService("TeleportService")
        local placeId = game.PlaceId
        local success, servers = pcall(function()
            return HttpService:JSONDecode(game:HttpGet("https://games.roblox.com/v1/games/"..placeId.."/servers/Public?sortOrder=Asc&limit=100"))
        end)
        if success and servers and servers.data then
            for _, v in pairs(servers.data) do
                if type(v) == "table" and v.maxPlayers > v.playing and v.id ~= game.JobId then
                    TPService:TeleportToPlaceInstance(placeId, v.id, game.Players.LocalPlayer)
                    break
                end
            end
        end
    end
end

-- ==========================================
-- LOGIC: AUTO ELITE HUNTER CÓ HOP SERVER
-- ==========================================
task.spawn(function()
    while task.wait(Sec or 0.1) do
        if _G.FarmEliteHunt then
            pcall(function()
                local plr = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                local replicated = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")
                local Enemies = workspace:FindFirstChild("Enemies")
                local questUI = plr.PlayerGui.Main.Quest

                -- Nếu ĐÃ CÓ nhiệm vụ
                if questUI.Visible == true then
                    local questText = questUI.Container.QuestTitle.Title.Text
                    if string.find(questText, "Diablo") or string.find(questText, "Urban") or string.find(questText, "Deandre") then
                        
                        -- Trang bị vũ khí trước khi đánh
                        if weaponSc and _G.ChooseWP then weaponSc(_G.ChooseWP) end

                        local foundElite = false
                        
                        -- 1. Check xem quái đã spawn vào map chưa
                        if Enemies then
                            for _, v in pairs(Enemies:GetChildren()) do
                                if (string.find(v.Name, "Diablo") or string.find(v.Name, "Urban") or string.find(v.Name, "Deandre")) then
                                    if v:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") and v.Humanoid.Health > 0 then
                                        foundElite = true
                                        repeat task.wait() 
                                            if v:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") and _tp then
                                                _tp(v.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame)
                                            end
                                            if Attack and Attack.Kill then 
                                                Attack.Kill(v, _G.FarmEliteHunt) 
                                            end
                                        until not _G.FarmEliteHunt or not questUI.Visible or not v.Parent or v.Humanoid.Health <= 0
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end

                        -- 2. Nếu quái chưa vào map, bay đi tìm ở các điểm spawn
                        if not foundElite then
                            for _, v in pairs(replicated:GetChildren()) do
                                if (string.find(v.Name, "Diablo") or string.find(v.Name, "Urban") or string.find(v.Name, "Deandre")) then
                                    if v:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") and _tp then
                                        _tp(v.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame)
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end
                        
                    end        
                else
                    -- CHƯA CÓ nhiệm vụ thì gọi remote để nhận
                    replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("EliteHunter")
                    task.wait(1) -- Chờ server phản hồi
                    
                    -- Nếu bật Hop và questUI vẫn không hiện (tức là NPC đang cooldown)
                    if _G.HopElite and not questUI.Visible then
                        if Fluent then
                            Fluent:Notify({
                                Title = "Elite Cooldown",
                                Content = "No Elite spawned. Hopping to another server...",
                                Duration = 3
                            })
                        end
                        task.wait(2)
                        HopServer()
                        task.wait(10) -- Nghỉ chờ load qua server mới
                    end
                end
            end)
        end
    end
end)

                local players = data.Count or data.Players or 0
                if bounty > best.Bounty and players < 12 then
                    best.JobId = jobId; best.Bounty = bounty; best.Players = players
                end

    end
    if best.JobId then
        RF:InvokeServer("teleport", best.JobId)

-- ==========================================
-- LOGIC: AUTO SOUL REAPER & HOP SERVER
-- ==========================================
task.spawn(function()
    while task.wait(Sec or 0.1) do
        if _G.AutoHytHallow then
            pcall(function()
                local plr = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                local commF = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").Remotes.CommF_
                local reaper = nil

                -- 1. Tìm Boss Soul Reaper trên map
                for _, v in pairs(workspace.Enemies:GetChildren()) do
                    if string.find(v.Name, "Soul Reaper") then
                        if v:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") and v.Humanoid.Health > 0 then
                            reaper = v
                            break
                        end
                    end
                end

                if reaper then
                    -- 2. Đã có Boss -> Bay lại chém
                    repeat task.wait()
                        -- Bay trên đầu boss 30 stud để né skill lưỡi hái
                        if reaper:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") and _tp then
                            _tp(reaper.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 30, 0))
                        end
                        if weaponSc and _G.ChooseWP then weaponSc(_G.ChooseWP) end
                        if Attack and Attack.Kill then Attack.Kill(reaper, _G.AutoHytHallow) end
                    until not _G.AutoHytHallow or not reaper.Parent or reaper.Humanoid.Health <= 0
                else
                    -- 3. Không có Boss -> Kiểm tra Balo tìm Hallow Essence
                    local essence = plr.Backpack:FindFirstChild("Hallow Essence") or (plr.Character and plr.Character:FindFirstChild("Hallow Essence"))

                    if essence then
                        -- Có Essence -> Bay lại bàn thờ (Altar)
                        local altarCFrame = CFrame.new(-8932.32, 146.83, 6062.55)
                        if _tp then _tp(altarCFrame) end
                        task.wait(0.5)
                        
                        -- Ép nhân vật tự cầm Essence lên tay để gọi Boss
                        if plr.Character and plr.Character:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") then
                            plr.Character.Humanoid:EquipTool(essence)
                        end
                    else
                        -- 4. Không có Boss & Không có Essence -> Xử lý Bones / Hop Server
                        local bonesCount = 0
                        if plr:FindFirstChild("Data") and plr.Data:FindFirstChild("Bones") then
                            bonesCount = plr.Data.Bones.Value
                        end

                        if bonesCount >= 50 then
                            -- Còn đủ Xương -> Tự động quay Random tại Death King
                            commF:InvokeServer("Bones", "Buy", 1, 1)
                            task.wait(0.5) -- Delay xíu chống spam lỗi game
                        else
                            -- Hết Xương (< 50) -> Nhảy Server nếu bật công tắc
                            if _G.HopSoulReaper then
                                if Fluent then
                                    Fluent:Notify({ 
                                        Title = "Soul Reaper Not Found", 
                                        Content = "No boss, no essence, and out of bones. Hopping...", 
                                        Duration = 3 
                                    })
                                end
                                task.wait(2)
                                HopServer()
                                task.wait(10)
                            end
                        end
                    end
                end
            end)
        end
    end
end)

-- ==========================================
-- LOGIC: AUTO ATTACK RIP INDRA & HOP SERVER
-- ==========================================
task.spawn(function()
    while task.wait(Sec or 0.1) do
        if _G.AutoRipIngay then
            pcall(function()
                local plr = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                local commF = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").Remotes.CommF_
                local indra = nil

                -- Tìm Boss bằng string.lower để không trượt
                for _, v in pairs(workspace.Enemies:GetChildren()) do
                    if string.find(string.lower(v.Name), "indra") then
                        if v:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") and v.Humanoid.Health > 0 then
                            indra = v
                            break
                        end
                    end
                end

                if indra then
                    -- Nếu chưa có đồ (Dark Dagger / Valkyrie) HOẶC boss đang sống -> Nhào vô đấm
                    repeat task.wait()
                        -- Cố định bay trên đầu 30 stud
                        if indra:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") and _tp then
                            _tp(indra.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 30, 0))
                        end
                        if weaponSc and _G.ChooseWP then weaponSc(_G.ChooseWP) end
                        if Attack and Attack.Kill then Attack.Kill(indra, _G.AutoRipIngay) end
                    until not _G.AutoRipIngay or not indra.Parent or indra.Humanoid.Health <= 0
                else
                    -- Không tìm thấy Boss
                    if _G.HopRipIndra then
                        -- Bật Hop thì nhảy server luôn
                        if Fluent then
                            Fluent:Notify({ 
                                Title = "Rip Indra Not Found", 
                                Content = "Boss is dead. Hopping to another server...", 
                                Duration = 3 
                            })
                        end
                        task.wait(2)
                        HopServer()
                        task.wait(10)
                    else
                        -- Không bật Hop thì bay về đỉnh tháp Castle chờ
                        -- Tọa độ entrance (Xin game phép dịch chuyển)
                        commF:InvokeServer("requestEntrance", Vector3.new(-5097.93, 316.44, -3142.66))
                        task.wait(0.5)
                        -- Bay lên mây chờ
                        if _tp then _tp(CFrame.new(-5344.82, 423.98, -2725.09)) end
                    end
                end
            end)
        end
    end
end)

    for i = 1, 100 do

                if bounty > best.Bounty and players < 12 then
                    best.JobId = jobId; best.Bounty = bounty; best.Players = players
                end
            end
        end
        task.wait()
    end
    if best.JobId then
        RF:InvokeServer("teleport", best.JobId)
    else
        local HttpService = game:GetService("HttpService")
        local TPService = game:GetService("TeleportService")
        local placeId = game.PlaceId
        local success, servers = pcall(function()
            return HttpService:JSONDecode(game:HttpGet("https://games.roblox.com/v1/games/"..placeId.."/servers/Public?sortOrder=Asc&limit=100"))
        end)
        if success and servers and servers.data then
            for _, v in pairs(servers.data) do
                if type(v) == "table" and v.maxPlayers > v.playing and v.id ~= game.JobId then
                    TPService:TeleportToPlaceInstance(placeId, v.id, game.Players.LocalPlayer)
                    break
                end

    end

task.spawn(function()
    while task.wait(Sec or 0.1) do
        if _G.AutoMiror then
            pcall(function()
                local doughKing = nil
                
                -- Tìm Boss bằng string.lower để không bị hụt tên
                for _, v in pairs(workspace.Enemies:GetChildren()) do
                    if string.find(string.lower(v.Name), "dough king") then
                        if v:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") and v.Humanoid.Health > 0 then
                            doughKing = v
                            break
                        end
                    end
                end

                if doughKing then
                    -- Có Boss -> Bay vào đấm
                    repeat task.wait()
                        -- Bay trên đầu 30 stud cho an toàn
                        if doughKing:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") and _tp then
                            _tp(doughKing.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 30, 0))
                        end
                        if weaponSc and _G.ChooseWP then weaponSc(_G.ChooseWP) end
                        if Attack and Attack.Kill then Attack.Kill(doughKing, _G.AutoMiror) end
                    until not _G.AutoMiror or not doughKing.Parent or doughKing.Humanoid.Health <= 0
                else
                    -- Không có Boss
                    if _G.HopDoughKing then
                        -- Nếu bật Hop thì nhảy server
                        if Fluent then
                            Fluent:Notify({ 
                                Title = "Dough King Not Found", 
                                Content = "Boss not spawned. Hopping to another server...", 
                                Duration = 3 
                            })
                        end
                        task.wait(2)
                        HopServer()
                        task.wait(10)
                    else
                        
                        if _tp then _tp(CFrame.new(-1943.676513671875, 251.5095672607422, -12337.880859375)) end
                    end
                end
            end)
        end
    end
end)

-- ==========================================
-- HÀM HỖ TRỢ (FUNCTIONS)
-- ==========================================
local function printBeltName(data) 
    if type(data) == "table" and data.Quest["BeltName"] then 
        return data.Quest["BeltName"] 
    end 
end

local function checkQuesta()
    local a = {[1] = {["Context"] = "Check"}}
    local b = nil
    pcall(function()
        local c = {[1] = {["Context"] = "RequestQuest"}}
        game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):WaitForChild("Modules"):WaitForChild("Net"):WaitForChild("RF/DragonHunter"):InvokeServer(unpack(c))
    end)
    local d, e = pcall(function()
        b = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):WaitForChild("Modules"):WaitForChild("Net"):WaitForChild("RF/DragonHunter"):InvokeServer(unpack(a))
    end)
    local f = false; local g; local h; local i
    if b then 
        if b.Text then 
            f = true
            local j = b.Text
            if string.find(tostring(j), "Defeat") then 
                i = 1
                g = string.sub(tostring(j), 8, 9)
                g = tonumber(g)
                local k = {"Hydra Enforcer", "Venomous Assailant"}
                for l, m in pairs(k) do 
                    if string.find(j, m) then h = m; break end 
                end 
            elseif string.find(tostring(j), "Destroy") then 
                g = 10; i = 2; h = nil 
            end 
        end 
    end
    return f, h, g, i 
end

local function BackTODoJo()
    for a, b in pairs(game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer.PlayerGui.Notifications:GetChildren()) do 
        if b.Name == "NotificationTemplate" then 
            if string.find(b.Text, "Head back to the Dojo to complete more tasks") then 
                return true 
            end 
        end 
    end
    return false 
end

local function DragonMobClear(a, b, c)
    if workspace.Enemies:FindFirstChild(b) then 
        for d, e in pairs(workspace.Enemies:GetChildren()) do 
            if e.Name == b and Attack.Alive(e) then 
                if a then Attack.Kill(e, a) end 
            end 
        end 
    else 
        if _tp then _tp(c) end
    end 
end

-- LOGIC 1: AUTO DOJO TRAINER
-- ==========================================
local dojoDebug = false
task.spawn(function()
    while task.wait(Sec or 0.1) do
        if _G.Dojoo then
            pcall(function()
                local plr = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                local Net = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").Modules.Net
                local args = {[1] = {["NPC"] = "Dojo Trainer", ["Command"] = "RequestQuest"}}        
                local progress = Net:FindFirstChild("RF/InteractDragonQuest"):InvokeServer(unpack(args))
                local NameBelt = printBeltName(progress)
                
                if dojoDebug == false and not progress and not NameBelt then
                    if _tp then _tp(CFrame.new(5865.02, 1208.31, 871.15)) end
                    dojoDebug = true
                elseif dojoDebug == true and (CFrame.new(5865.02, 1208.31, 871.15).Position - plr.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position).Magnitude <= 50 then
                    if NameBelt == "White" then
                        local v = GetConnectionEnemies("Skull Slayer")
                        if v then 
                            repeat task.wait() Attack.Kill(v, _G.Dojoo) until not progress or not _G.Dojoo or not Attack.Alive(v)
                        else 
                            if _tp then _tp(CFrame.new(-16759.58, 71.28, 1595.33)) end
                        end
                    elseif NameBelt == "Yellow" then
                        repeat task.wait()
                            _G.SeaBeast1, _G.TerrorShark, _G.Shark, _G.Piranha, _G.MobCrew, _G.FishBoat, _G.SailBoats = true, true, true, true, true, true, true
                        until not _G.Dojoo or not progress
                        _G.SeaBeast1, _G.TerrorShark, _G.Shark, _G.Piranha, _G.MobCrew, _G.FishBoat, _G.SailBoats = false, false, false, false, false, false, false
                    elseif NameBelt == "Green" then
                        repeat task.wait() _G.SailBoats = true until not _G.Dojoo or not progress
                        _G.SailBoats = false
                    elseif NameBelt == "Purple" then
                        repeat task.wait() _G.FarmEliteHunt = true until not _G.Dojoo or not progress
                        _G.FarmEliteHunt = false
                    elseif NameBelt == "Red" then
                        repeat task.wait() _G.SailBoats, _G.FishBoat = true, true until not _G.Dojoo or not progress
                        _G.SailBoats, _G.FishBoat = false, false                      
                    elseif NameBelt == "Black" then
                        repeat task.wait()              
                            if workspace.Map:FindFirstChild("PrehistoricIsland") or workspace._WorldOrigin.Locations:FindFirstChild("Prehistoric Island") then    
                                _G.Prehis_Find = true                   
                                if workspace.Map.PrehistoricIsland.Core.ActivationPrompt:FindFirstChild("ProximityPrompt", true) then
                                    _G.Prehis_Skills, _G.Prehis_Find = false, true
                                else
                                    _G.Prehis_Skills, _G.Prehis_Find = true, false
                                end
                            else
                                _G.Prehis_Find, _G.Prehis_Skills = true, false
                            end
                        until not _G.Dojoo or not progress
                        _G.Prehis_Find, _G.Prehis_Skills = false, false                        
                    elseif NameBelt == "Orange" or NameBelt == "Blue" then
                        return nil
                    end
                end
                
                if not progress then
                    dojoDebug = false
                    local argsClaim = {[1] = {["NPC"] = "Dojo Trainer", ["Command"] = "ClaimQuest"}}
                    Net:FindFirstChild("RF/InteractDragonQuest"):InvokeServer(unpack(argsClaim))
                end
            end)
        end
    end
end)

        if _G.FarmBlazeEM then

                local a, v, h, x = checkQuesta()                  
                if a == true and not BackTODoJo() then
                    if x == 1 then
                        if v == "Hydra Enforcer" or v == "Venomous Assailant" then            
                            repeat task.wait()
                                DragonMobClear(true, v, CFrame.new(4620.61, 1002.29, 399.08))
                            until not _G.FarmBlazeEM or not a or BackTODoJo()                            
                        end      
                    elseif x == 2 then
                        local bamboo = workspace.Map.Waterfall.IslandModel:FindFirstChild("Meshes/bambootree", true)
                        if bamboo then
                            repeat task.wait()                
                                if _tp then _tp(bamboo.CFrame * CFrame.new(4, 0, 0)) end
                                local Root = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                                if Root and (bamboo.Position - Root.Position).Magnitude <= 200 then
                                    MousePos = bamboo.Position
                                    if Useskills then
                                        Useskills("Melee","Z"); Useskills("Melee","X"); Useskills("Melee","C"); task.wait(0.5)
                                        Useskills("Sword","Z"); Useskills("Sword","X"); task.wait(0.5)
                                        Useskills("Blox Fruit","Z"); Useskills("Blox Fruit","X"); Useskills("Blox Fruit","C"); task.wait(0.5)
                                        Useskills("Gun","Z"); Useskills("Gun","X")
                                    end
                                end
                            until not _G.FarmBlazeEM or not a or BackTODoJo()
                        end
                    end
                else
                    if _tp then _tp(CFrame.new(5813, 1208, 884)) end
                    DragonMobClear(false, nil, nil) 
                end
            end)
        end
    end
end)

local HopChest = Tabs.FarmingOther:AddToggle("HopChest", {
    Title = "Auto Hop Chest", 
    Description = "Automatically hop server when all chests are collected", 
    Default = false
})
HopChest:OnChanged(function(Value)
    _G.AutoHopChest = Value
end)

-- ==========================================
-- LOGIC: HOP SERVER (Có thể xóa đoạn func này nếu bro đã khai báo ở các đoạn code trên)
-- ==========================================
local function HopServer()
    local RF = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):WaitForChild("__ServerBrowser")
    local best = { Bounty = 0, JobId = nil }
    for i = 1, 100 do
        local ok, res = pcall(RF.InvokeServer, RF, i)
        if ok and typeof(res) == "table" then
            for jobId, data in pairs(res) do
                local bounty = tonumber(data.Bounty) or 0
                local players = data.Count or data.Players or 0
                if bounty > best.Bounty and players < 12 then
                    best.JobId = jobId; best.Bounty = bounty; best.Players = players
                end
            end
        end
        task.wait()
    end
    if best.JobId then
        RF:InvokeServer("teleport", best.JobId)
    else
        local HttpService = game:GetService("HttpService")
        local TPService = game:GetService("TeleportService")
        local placeId = game.PlaceId
        local success, servers = pcall(function()
            return HttpService:JSONDecode(game:HttpGet("https://games.roblox.com/v1/games/"..placeId.."/servers/Public?sortOrder=Asc&limit=100"))
        end)
        if success and servers and servers.data then
            for _, v in pairs(servers.data) do
                if type(v) == "table" and v.maxPlayers > v.playing and v.id ~= game.JobId then
                    TPService:TeleportToPlaceInstance(placeId, v.id, game.Players.LocalPlayer)
                    break
                end
            end
        end
    end
end

-- ==========================================
-- LOGIC: AUTO FARM CHEST & HOP SERVER
-- ==========================================
task.spawn(function()
    while task.wait(Sec or 0.1) do
        if _G.AutoFarmChest then
            pcall(function()
                local CollectionService = game:GetService("CollectionService")
                local Players = game:GetService("Players")
                local Player = Players.LocalPlayer
                local Character = Player.Character
                if not Character or not Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then return end
                
                local Position = Character:GetPivot().Position
                local Chests = CollectionService:GetTagged("_ChestTagged")      
                local Distance, Nearest = math.huge, nil  
                
                -- Tìm rương gần nhất
                for i = 1, #Chests do
                    local ChestObj = Chests[i]
                    if ChestObj and ChestObj.Parent then
                        local Magnitude = (ChestObj:GetPivot().Position - Position).Magnitude        
                        if not SelectedIsland or ChestObj:IsDescendantOf(SelectedIsland) then
                            if not ChestObj:GetAttribute("IsDisabled") and Magnitude < Distance then
                                Distance = Magnitude
                                Nearest = ChestObj
                            end
                        end
                    end
                end
                
                if Nearest then 
                    -- Nếu tìm thấy rương -> Bay lại nhặt
                    if _tp then _tp(Nearest:GetPivot()) end
                else
                    -- Nếu map sạch bóng rương -> Tiến hành kiểm tra Hop Server
                    if _G.AutoHopChest then
                        if Fluent then
                            Fluent:Notify({ 
                                Title = "Chests Cleared", 
                                Content = "No more chests found. Hopping server...", 
                                Duration = 3 
                            })
                        end
                        task.wait(2)
                        HopServer()
                        task.wait(10)
                    end
                end
            end)
        end
    end
end)

-- LOGIC: HOP SERVER (Có thể xóa đoạn func này nếu bro đã khai báo ở các đoạn code trước)
-- ==========================================
local function HopServer()
    local RF = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):WaitForChild("__ServerBrowser")
    local best = { Bounty = 0, JobId = nil }
    for i = 1, 100 do
        local ok, res = pcall(RF.InvokeServer, RF, i)
        if ok and typeof(res) == "table" then
            for jobId, data in pairs(res) do
                local bounty = tonumber(data.Bounty) or 0
                local players = data.Count or data.Players or 0
                if bounty > best.Bounty and players < 12 then
                    best.JobId = jobId; best.Bounty = bounty; best.Players = players
                end
            end
        end
        task.wait()
    end
    if best.JobId then
        RF:InvokeServer("teleport", best.JobId)
    else
        local HttpService = game:GetService("HttpService")
        local TPService = game:GetService("TeleportService")
        local placeId = game.PlaceId
        local success, servers = pcall(function()
            return HttpService:JSONDecode(game:HttpGet("https://games.roblox.com/v1/games/"..placeId.."/servers/Public?sortOrder=Asc&limit=100"))
        end)
        if success and servers and servers.data then
            for _, v in pairs(servers.data) do
                if type(v) == "table" and v.maxPlayers > v.playing and v.id ~= game.JobId then
                    TPService:TeleportToPlaceInstance(placeId, v.id, game.Players.LocalPlayer)
                    break
                end
            end
        end
    end
end

-- ==========================================
-- LOGIC: AUTO COLLECT BERRY & HOP SERVER
-- ==========================================
task.spawn(function()
    while task.wait(Sec or 0.1) do
        if _G.AutoBerry then
            pcall(function()
                local CollectionService = game:GetService("CollectionService")
                local BerryBush = CollectionService:GetTagged("BerryBush")      
                local foundBerry = false
                
                -- Vòng lặp quét các bụi dâu
                for i = 1, #BerryBush do
                    if not _G.AutoBerry then return end
                    local Bush = BerryBush[i]        
                    
                    if Bush and Bush.Parent then
                        -- Kiểm tra thuộc tính của bụi cây xem có quả không
                        for AttributeName, BerryName in pairs(Bush:GetAttributes()) do
                            if not BerryArray or table.find(BerryArray, BerryName) then           
                                -- Bay đến vị trí bụi cây gốc
                                if _tp then _tp(Bush.Parent:GetPivot()) end
                                task.wait(0.1)
                                
                                -- Quét các quả nằm bên trong bụi cây để thu hoạch
                                for _, child in pairs(Bush:GetChildren()) do
                                    if not BerryArray or table.find(BerryArray, child.Name) then
                                        if child:IsA("BasePart") and child:FindFirstChildOfClass("ProximityPrompt") then
                                            foundBerry = true
                                            -- Bay thẳng vào quả dâu
                                            if _tp then _tp(child.WorldPivot) end
                                            task.wait(0.1)
                                            -- Kích hoạt nhặt quả dâu
                                            fireproximityprompt(child:FindFirstChildOfClass("ProximityPrompt"), math.huge)
                                        end
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    end
                end
                
                -- Nếu đi hết vòng lặp mà không hái được quả nào (Hết sạch dâu trên map)
                if not foundBerry then
                    if _G.AutoHopBerry then
                        if Fluent then
                            Fluent:Notify({ 
                                Title = "Berries Cleared", 
                                Content = "No more berries found. Hopping server...", 
                                Duration = 3 
                            })
                        end
                        task.wait(2)
                        HopServer()
                        task.wait(10)
                    end
                end
            end)
        end
    end
end)

        _G.SelectChip = Value
    end
})

    Title = "Auto Select Dungeon Chip",
    Description = "Auto switch chip based on fruit in inventory",

        _G.AutoSelectDungeon = Value
    end
})

Tabs.FruitAndRaid:AddButton({
    Title = "Buy Dungeon Chips [Beli]",
    Description = "Buy normal chip using money",
    Callback = function()
        if not GetBP("Special Microchip") then 
            CommF:InvokeServer("RaidsNpc", "Select", _G.SelectChip) 
        end
    end
})

Tabs.FruitAndRaid:AddButton({
    Title = "Buy Dungeon Chips [Devil Fruit]",
    Description = "Use your lowest fruit under 490k Beli",
    Callback = function()
        if GetBP("Special Microchip") then return end
        local FruitPrice = {}
        for i, v in next, CommF:InvokeServer("GetFruits") do
            if v.Price <= 490000 then 
                table.insert(FruitPrice, v.Name) 
            end 
        end    
        for _, y in pairs(FruitPrice) do    
            for _, v in pairs(DungeonTables) do 
                if not GetBP("Special Microchip") then     
                    CommF:InvokeServer("LoadFruit", tostring(y))	      
                    CommF:InvokeServer("RaidsNpc", "Select", _G.SelectChip)	
                end            
            end    
        end
    end
})

-- ==========================================
-- THREADS LOGIC PROCESSING
-- ==========================================

-- 1. Auto Select Chip Logic
task.spawn(function()
    while task.wait(Sec or 0.5) do
        if _G.AutoSelectDungeon then
            pcall(function()
                if GetBP("Flame-Flame") then _G.SelectChip = "Flame"
                elseif GetBP("Ice-Ice") then _G.SelectChip = "Ice"
                elseif GetBP("Quake-Quake") then _G.SelectChip = "Quake"
                elseif GetBP("Light-Light") then _G.SelectChip = "Light"
                elseif GetBP("Dark-Dark") then _G.SelectChip = "Dark"
                elseif GetBP("String-String") then _G.SelectChip = "String"
                elseif GetBP("Rumble-Rumble") then _G.SelectChip = "Rumble"
                elseif GetBP("Magma-Magma") then _G.SelectChip = "Magma"
                elseif GetBP("Human-Human: Buddha Fruit") then _G.SelectChip = "Human: Buddha"
                elseif GetBP("Dough-Dough") then _G.SelectChip = "Dough"
                elseif GetBP("Sand-Sand") then _G.SelectChip = "Sand"
                elseif GetBP("Bird-Bird: Phoenix") then _G.SelectChip = "Bird: Phoenix"
                else _G.SelectChip = "Ice" end
            end)
        end
    end
end)

-- 2. Auto Start Raid Button Clicker
task.spawn(function()
    while task.wait(Sec or 0.5) do
        if _G.Auto_StartRaid then
            pcall(function()
                if plr.PlayerGui.Main.TopHUDList.RaidTimer.Visible == false and GetBP("Special Microchip") then
                    if World2 then
                        if _tp then _tp(CFrame.new(-6438.73, 250.64, -4501.50)) end
                        fireclickdetector(workspace.Map.CircleIsland.RaidSummon2.Button.Main.ClickDetector)
                    elseif World3 then                   
                        CommF:InvokeServer("requestEntrance", Vector3.new(-5097.93, 316.44, -3142.66))
                        fireclickdetector(workspace.Map["Boat Castle"].RaidSummon2.Button.Main.ClickDetector)
                    end
                end
            end)
        end
    end
end)    

-- 3. Auto Kill Enemies in Stages
task.spawn(function()
    while task.wait(Sec or 0.1) do
        if _G.Raiding then  
            pcall(function()
                if plr.PlayerGui.Main.TopHUDList.RaidTimer.Visible == true then          
                    local islands = {"Island5", "Island 4", "Island 3", "Island 2", "Island 1"}
                    for _, island in ipairs(islands) do
                        local location = game:GetService("Workspace")["_WorldOrigin"].Locations:FindFirstChild(island)
                        if location then
                            for _, v in pairs(workspace.Enemies:GetChildren()) do
                                if v:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") and v.Humanoid.Health > 0 then
                                    repeat task.wait() 
                                        Attack.Kill(v, _G.Raiding) 
                                        NextIs = false 
                                    until not _G.Raiding or not v.Parent or v.Humanoid.Health <= 0 
                                    NextIs = true
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    end
                else
                    NextIs = false
                end
            end)
        else
            NextIs = false
        end
    end
end)

-- 4. Kill Aura Logic
task.spawn(function()
    while task.wait(Sec or 0.1) do
        if _G.KillH then
            for _, v in pairs(workspace.Enemies:GetChildren()) do
                if Attack.Alive(v) then
                    pcall(function()
                        repeat task.wait(Sec or 0.1)
                            sethiddenproperty(plr, "SimulationRadius", math.huge)
                            v:BreakJoints()
                            v.Humanoid.Health = 0
                            if v:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then 
                                v.HumanoidRootPart.CanCollide = false 
                            end
                        until not _G.KillH or not v.Parent or v.Humanoid.Health <= 0
                    end)
                end
            end
        end
    end
end)

-- 5. Auto Next Island TP Sky Zone
task.spawn(function()
    while task.wait(Sec or 0.2) do
        if NextIs and _tp then
            pcall(function()
                if plr.PlayerGui.Main.TopHUDList.RaidTimer.Visible == true then
                    local locs = game:GetService("Workspace")["_WorldOrigin"].Locations
                    if locs:FindFirstChild("Island 5") then _tp(locs["Island 5"].CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 50, 100))
                    elseif locs:FindFirstChild("Island 4") then _tp(locs["Island 4"].CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 50, 100))
                    elseif locs:FindFirstChild("Island 3") then _tp(locs["Island 3"].CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 50, 100))
                    elseif locs:FindFirstChild("Island 2") then _tp(locs["Island 2"].CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 50, 100))
                    elseif locs:FindFirstChild("Island 1") then _tp(locs["Island 1"].CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 50, 100))
                    end
                end
            end)
        end
    end
end)

-- 6. Auto Awakener Interaction
task.spawn(function()
    while task.wait(Sec or 1) do
        if _G.Auto_Awakener then
            pcall(function()
                CommF:InvokeServer("Awakener", "Check")
                CommF:InvokeServer("Awakener", "Awaken")
            end)
        end
    end
end)

-- ==========================================
-- THREADS REAL-TIME TRACKING & LOGIC
-- ==========================================

-- 1. Real-time Status Tracker (Spy, Frozen, Kitsune Status)
task.spawn(function()
    while task.wait(0.2) do
        pcall(function()
            -- Spy Status
            local spycheck = string.match(CommF:InvokeServer("InfoLeviathan", "1"), "%d+")
            if spycheck then 
                if tostring(spycheck) == "5" then
                    SPYING:SetDesc(" Spy Leviathan : Already Done!!")
                else
                    SPYING:SetDesc(" Spy Leviathan  : " .. tostring(spycheck))
                end
            end
            
            -- Frozen Dimension Status
            if workspace._WorldOrigin.Locations:FindFirstChild('Frozen Dimension') then
                FloD:SetDesc(' Flozen Dimension : True')
            else
                FloD:SetDesc(' Flozen Dimension : False')
            end

            -- Kitsune Status
            if workspace.Map:FindFirstChild("KitsuneIsland") or workspace._WorldOrigin.Locations:FindFirstChild("Kitsune Island") then
                Check_Kitsu:SetDesc(" Kitsune Island : True")
            else
                Check_Kitsu:SetDesc(" Kitsune Island : False")
            end
        end)
    end
end)

-- 2. Leviathan Gate Teleport Thread
task.spawn(function()
    while task.wait(0.1) do
        if _G.FrozenTP then
            pcall(function()
                if workspace.Map:FindFirstChild("LeviathanGate") and _tp then 
                    _tp(workspace.Map.LeviathanGate.CFrame) 
                    game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):WaitForChild("Remotes"):WaitForChild("CommF_"):InvokeServer("OpenLeviathanGate") 
                end
            end)
        end
    end
end)

-- 3. Auto Sail Hydra Island Thread
task.spawn(function()
    while task.wait() do
        if _G.SailBoat_Hydra then 
            pcall(function()        
                local myBoat = CheckBoat()
                if not myBoat then
                    local buyBoatCFrame = CFrame.new(-16927.451, 9.086, 433.864)
                    if TeleportToTarget then TeleportToTarget(buyBoatCFrame) end
                    if (buyBoatCFrame.Position - plr.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position).Magnitude <= 10 then CommF:InvokeServer("BuyBoat", _G.SelectedBoat) end
                elseif myBoat then
                    if plr.Character.Humanoid.Sit == false then
                        if _tp then _tp(myBoat.VehicleSeat.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 1, 0)) end
                    else                         
                        repeat task.wait() 
                            if CheckEnemiesBoat() or CheckPirateGrandBrigade() or CheckTerrorShark() then
                                if _tp then _tp(CFrame.new(5433, 150, 290)) end
                            else
                                if _tp then _tp(CFrame.new(5433, 35, 290)) end
                            end           
                        until _G.SailBoat_Hydra == false or plr.Character:WaitForChild("Humanoid").Sit == false 
                        plr.Character.Humanoid.Sit = false
                    end
                end
            end)
        end
    end
end)

-- 4. Main Auto Sail Danger Level Thread
task.spawn(function()
    while task.wait() do
        if _G.SailBoats then 
            pcall(function()        
                local myBoat = CheckBoat()
                local isEventSpawning = (CheckShark() and _G.Shark or CheckTerrorShark() and _G.TerrorShark or CheckFishCrew() and _G.MobCrew or CheckPiranha() and _G.Piranha) or (CheckEnemiesBoat() and _G.FishBoat) or (CheckSeaBeast() and _G.SeaBeast1) or (_G.PGB and CheckPirateGrandBrigade()) or (_G.HCM and CheckHauntedCrew()) or (_G.Leviathan1 and CheckLeviathan())
                
                if not myBoat and not isEventSpawning then
                    local buyBoatCFrame = CFrame.new(-16927.451, 9.086, 433.864)
                    if TeleportToTarget then TeleportToTarget(buyBoatCFrame) end
                    if (buyBoatCFrame.Position - plr.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position).Magnitude <= 10 then CommF:InvokeServer("BuyBoat", _G.SelectedBoat) end
                elseif myBoat and not isEventSpawning then
                    if plr.Character.Humanoid.Sit == false then
                        if _tp then _tp(myBoat.VehicleSeat.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 1, 0)) end
                    else                         
                        local CFrameSelectedZone
                        if _G.DangerSc == "Lv 1" then CFrameSelectedZone = CFrame.new(-21998.37, 30.00, -682.30)
                        elseif _G.DangerSc == "Lv 2" then CFrameSelectedZone = CFrame.new(-26779.52, 30.00, -822.85)
                        elseif _G.DangerSc == "Lv 3" then CFrameSelectedZone = CFrame.new(-31171.95, 30.00, -2256.93)
                        elseif _G.DangerSc == "Lv 4" then CFrameSelectedZone = CFrame.new(-34054.68, 30.21, -2560.12)
                        elseif _G.DangerSc == "Lv 5" then CFrameSelectedZone = CFrame.new(-38887.55, 30.00, -2162.99)
                        elseif _G.DangerSc == "Lv 6" then CFrameSelectedZone = CFrame.new(-44541.76, 30.00, -1244.85)
                        elseif _G.DangerSc == "Lv Infinite" then CFrameSelectedZone = CFrame.new(-10000000, 31, 37016.25)
                        end           
                        
                        repeat task.wait() 
                            if (not _G.FishBoat and CheckEnemiesBoat()) or (not _G.PGB and CheckPirateGrandBrigade()) or (not _G.TerrorShark and CheckTerrorShark()) then
                                if _tp then _tp(CFrameSelectedZone * CFrame.new(0, 150, 0)) end
                            else
                                if _tp then _tp(CFrameSelectedZone) end
                            end           
                        until _G.SailBoats == false or (CheckShark() and _G.Shark or CheckTerrorShark() and _G.TerrorShark or CheckFishCrew() and _G.MobCrew or CheckPiranha() and _G.Piranha) or CheckSeaBeast() and _G.SeaBeast1 or CheckEnemiesBoat() and _G.FishBoat or _G.Leviathan1 and CheckLeviathan() or _G.HCM and CheckHauntedCrew() or _G.PGB and CheckPirateGrandBrigade() or plr.Character:WaitForChild("Humanoid").Sit == false 
                        plr.Character.Humanoid.Sit = false
                    end
                end
            end)
        end
    end
end)

-- 5. No Collision for Boats
task.spawn(function()
    while task.wait(Sec or 0.5) do 
        pcall(function()
            for _, b in pairs(workspace.Boats:GetChildren()) do
                for _, d in pairs(b:GetDescendants()) do 
                    if d:IsA("BasePart") then 
                        if _G.SailBoats or _G.Prehis_Find or _G.FindMirage or _G.SailBoat_Hydra or _G.AutofindKitIs then 
                            d.CanCollide = false 
                        else 
                            d.CanCollide = true 
                        end 
                    end 
                end 
            end 
        end)
    end 
end)

-- 6. Main Combat Logic for Entities
task.spawn(function()
    while task.wait() do
        pcall(function()	
            if _G.Shark and CheckShark() then 
                for _, c in pairs(workspace.Enemies:GetChildren()) do 
                    if c.Name == "Shark" and Attack.Alive(c) then 
                        repeat task.wait() Attack.Kill(c, _G.Shark) until _G.Shark == false or not c.Parent or c.Humanoid.Health <= 0 
                    end 
                end 
            end
            if _G.TerrorShark and CheckTerrorShark() then 
                for _, c in pairs(workspace.Enemies:GetChildren()) do 
                    if c.Name == "Terrorshark" and Attack.Alive(c) then 
                        repeat task.wait() Attack.KillSea(c, _G.TerrorShark) until _G.TerrorShark == false or not c.Parent or c.Humanoid.Health <= 0 
                    end 
                end 
            end
            if _G.Piranha and CheckPiranha() then 
                for _, c in pairs(workspace.Enemies:GetChildren()) do 
                    if c.Name == "Piranha" and Attack.Alive(c) then 
                        repeat task.wait() Attack.Kill(c, _G.Piranha) until _G.Piranha == false or not c.Parent or c.Humanoid.Health <= 0 
                    end 
                end 
            end
            if _G.MobCrew and CheckFishCrew() then 
                for _, c in pairs(workspace.Enemies:GetChildren()) do 
                    if c.Name == "Fish Crew Member" and Attack.Alive(c) then 
                        repeat task.wait() Attack.Kill(c, _G.MobCrew) until _G.MobCrew == false or not c.Parent or c.Humanoid.Health <= 0 
                    end 
                end 
            end                 
            if _G.HCM and CheckHauntedCrew() then 
                for _, c in pairs(workspace.Enemies:GetChildren()) do 
                    if c.Name == "Haunted Crew Member" and Attack.Alive(c) then 
                        repeat task.wait() Attack.Kill(c, _G.HCM) until _G.HCM == false or not c.Parent or c.Humanoid.Health <= 0 
                    end 
                end 
            end
            if _G.SeaBeast1 and workspace.SeaBeasts:FindFirstChild("SeaBeast1") then 
                for _, b in pairs(workspace.SeaBeasts:GetChildren()) do 
                    if b:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") and b:FindFirstChild("Health") and b.Health.Value > 0 then 
                        repeat task.wait() 
                            task.spawn(function() if _tp then _tp(CFrame.new(b.HumanoidRootPart.Position.X, workspace.Map["WaterBase-Plane"].Position.Y + 200, b.HumanoidRootPart.Position.Z)) end end)
                            if plr:DistanceFromCharacter(b.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame.Position) <= 500 then 
                                AitSeaSkill_Custom = b.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame; MousePos = AitSeaSkill_Custom.Position;
                                if CheckF() then 
                                    weaponSc("Blox Fruit") Useskills("Blox Fruit","Z") Useskills("Blox Fruit","X") Useskills("Blox Fruit","C")
                                else 
                                    Useskills("Melee","Z") Useskills("Melee","X") Useskills("Melee","C") task.wait(0.1)
                                    Useskills("Sword","Z") Useskills("Sword","X") task.wait(0.1)
                                    Useskills("Blox Fruit","Z") Useskills("Blox Fruit","X") Useskills("Blox Fruit","C") task.wait(0.1)
                                    Useskills("Gun","Z") Useskills("Gun","X")
                                end 
                            end 
                        until _G.SeaBeast1 == false or not b:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") or not b.Parent or b.Health.Value <= 0 
                    end 
                end 
            end
            if _G.Leviathan1 and workspace.SeaBeasts:FindFirstChild("Leviathan") then 
                for _, b in pairs(workspace.SeaBeasts:GetChildren()) do 
                    if b:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") and b:FindFirstChild("Leviathan Segment") and b:FindFirstChild("Health") and b.Health.Value > 0 then 
                        repeat task.wait() 
                            task.spawn(function() if _tp then _tp(CFrame.new(b.HumanoidRootPart.Position.X, workspace.Map["WaterBase-Plane"].Position.Y + 200, b.HumanoidRootPart.Position.Z)) end end)
                            if plr:DistanceFromCharacter(b.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame.Position) <= 500 then 
                                MousePos = b:FindFirstChild("Leviathan Segment").Position;
                                if CheckF() then 
                                    weaponSc("Blox Fruit") Useskills("Blox Fruit","Z") Useskills("Blox Fruit","X") Useskills("Blox Fruit","C")
                                else 
                                    Useskills("Melee","Z") Useskills("Melee","X") Useskills("Melee","C") task.wait(0.1)
                                    Useskills("Sword","Z") Useskills("Sword","X") task.wait(0.1)
                                    Useskills("Blox Fruit","Z") Useskills("Blox Fruit","X") Useskills("Blox Fruit","C") task.wait(0.1)
                                    Useskills("Gun","Z") Useskills("Gun","X")
                                end 
                            end 
                        until _G.Leviathan1 == false or not b:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") or not b.Parent or b.Health.Value <= 0 
                    end 
                end 
            end
            if _G.FishBoat and CheckEnemiesBoat() then 
                for _, b in pairs(workspace.Enemies:GetChildren()) do 
                    if b:FindFirstChild("Health") and b.Health.Value > 0 and b:FindFirstChild("VehicleSeat") then 
                        repeat task.wait() 
                            task.spawn(function() if b.Name == "FishBoat" and _tp then _tp(b.Engine.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, -50, -25)) end end)
                            if plr:DistanceFromCharacter(b.Engine.CFrame.Position) <= 150 then 
                                AitSeaSkill_Custom = b.Engine.CFrame; MousePos = AitSeaSkill_Custom.Position;
                                if CheckF() then 
                                    weaponSc("Blox Fruit") Useskills("Blox Fruit","Z") Useskills("Blox Fruit","X") Useskills("Blox Fruit","C")
                                else 
                                    Useskills("Melee","Z") Useskills("Melee","X") Useskills("Melee","C") task.wait(0.1)
                                    Useskills("Sword","Z") Useskills("Sword","X") task.wait(0.1)
                                    Useskills("Blox Fruit","Z") Useskills("Blox Fruit","X") Useskills("Blox Fruit","C") task.wait(0.1)
                                    Useskills("Gun","Z") Useskills("Gun","X")
                                end 
                            end 
                        until _G.FishBoat == false or not b:FindFirstChild("VehicleSeat") or b.Health.Value <= 0 
                    end 
                end 
            end
            if _G.PGB and CheckPirateGrandBrigade() then 
                for _, b in pairs(workspace.Enemies:GetChildren()) do 
                    if b:FindFirstChild("Health") and b.Health.Value > 0 and b:FindFirstChild("VehicleSeat") then 
                        repeat task.wait() 
                            task.spawn(function()
                                if not _tp then return end
                                if b.Name == "PirateBrigade" then _tp(b.Engine.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, -30, -10))
                                elseif b.Name == "PirateGrandBrigade" then _tp(b.Engine.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, -50, -50)) end 
                            end)
                            if plr:DistanceFromCharacter(b.Engine.CFrame.Position) <= 150 then 
                                AitSeaSkill_Custom = b.Engine.CFrame; MousePos = AitSeaSkill_Custom.Position;
                                if CheckF() then 
                                    weaponSc("Blox Fruit") Useskills("Blox Fruit","Z") Useskills("Blox Fruit","X") Useskills("Blox Fruit","C")
                                else 
                                    Useskills("Melee","Z") Useskills("Melee","X") Useskills("Melee","C") task.wait(0.1)
                                    Useskills("Sword","Z") Useskills("Sword","X") task.wait(0.1)
                                    Useskills("Blox Fruit","Z") Useskills("Blox Fruit","X") Useskills("Blox Fruit","C") task.wait(0.1)
                                    Useskills("Gun","Z") Useskills("Gun","X")
                                end 
                            end 
                        until _G.PGB == false or not b:FindFirstChild("VehicleSeat") or b.Health.Value <= 0 
                    end 
                end 
            end
        end)
    end
end)

-- 7. Auto Find Kitsune Island Logic Thread
task.spawn(function()
    while task.wait() do
        if _G.AutofindKitIs then 
            pcall(function()
                if not workspace["_WorldOrigin"].Locations:FindFirstChild("Kitsune Island", true) then                
                    local myBoat = CheckBoat()
                    if not myBoat then
                        local buyBoatCFrame = CFrame.new(-16927.451, 9.086, 433.864)
                        if TeleportToTarget then TeleportToTarget(buyBoatCFrame) end
                        if (buyBoatCFrame.Position - plr.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position).Magnitude <= 10 then CommF:InvokeServer("BuyBoat", _G.SelectedBoat) end
                    else
                        if plr.Character.Humanoid.Sit == false then
                            if _tp then _tp(myBoat.VehicleSeat.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 1, 0)) end
                        else
                            local targetDestination = CFrame.new(-10000000, 31, 37016.25)              
                            repeat task.wait() 
                                if CheckEnemiesBoat() or CheckTerrorShark() or CheckPirateGrandBrigade() then
                                    if _tp then _tp(CFrame.new(-10000000, 150, 37016.25)) end
                                else
                                    if _tp then _tp(CFrame.new(-10000000, 31, 37016.25)) end
                                end
                            until not _G.AutofindKitIs or (targetDestination.Position - plr.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position).Magnitude <= 10 or workspace["_WorldOrigin"].Locations:FindFirstChild("Kitsune Island") or plr.Character.Humanoid.Sit == false 
                            plr.Character.Humanoid.Sit = false
                        end
                    end
                else
                    if _tp then _tp(workspace._WorldOrigin.Locations:FindFirstChild("Kitsune Island").CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 500, 0)) end
                end
            end)
        end
    end
end)

-- 8. Auto Tween Shrine Active Thread
task.spawn(function()
    while task.wait(0.1) do
        if _G.tweenShrine then
            pcall(function()
                local kit_is = workspace.Map:FindFirstChild("KitsuneIsland") or game.Workspace._WorldOrigin.Locations:FindFirstChild("Kitsune Island")
                local shrineActive = kit_is and kit_is:FindFirstChild("ShrineActive")
                if shrineActive then
                    for _, v in next, shrineActive:GetDescendants() do
                        if v:IsA("BasePart") and v.Name:find("NeonShrinePart") then
                            if Net:FindFirstChild("RE/TouchKitsuneStatue") then Net["RE/TouchKitsuneStatue"]:FireServer() end
                            repeat task.wait() if _tp then _tp(v.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 2, 0)) end until _G.tweenShrine == false or not kit_is
                        end
                    end
                else
                    if _tp then _tp(workspace._WorldOrigin.Locations:FindFirstChild("Kitsune Island").CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 500, 0)) end        
                end
            end)
        end
    end
end)

-- 9. Auto Collect Azure Ember Thread
task.spawn(function()
    while task.wait(0.1) do
        if _G.Collect_Ember then
            pcall(function()
                if workspace:WaitForChild("AttachedAzureEmber", 1) or workspace:WaitForChild("EmberTemplate", 1) then
                    local targetEmber = workspace:FindFirstChild("EmberTemplate")
                    if targetEmber and targetEmber:FindFirstChild("Part") and notween then 
                        notween(targetEmber.Part.CFrame) 
                    end
                else
                    if _tp then _tp(workspace._WorldOrigin.Locations:FindFirstChild("Kitsune Island").CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 500, 0)) end        
                    if Net:FindFirstChild("RF/KitsuneStatuePray") then Net["RF/KitsuneStatuePray"]:InvokeServer() end
                end
            end)
        end
    end
end)

-- 10. Auto Trade Azure Ember Thread
task.spawn(function()
    while task.wait(0.1) do
        if _G.Trade_Ember then
            pcall(function()
                if workspace["_WorldOrigin"].Locations:FindFirstChild("Kitsune Island", true) then
                    if Net:FindFirstChild("RF/KitsuneStatuePray") then Net["RF/KitsuneStatuePray"]:InvokeServer() end
                end
            end)
        end
    end
end)

-- THREADS REAL-TIME TRACKING & LOGIC

-- 1. Mirage Island Status Tracker
task.spawn(function()
    while task.wait(0.2) do
        if workspace.Map:FindFirstChild("MysticIsland") or workspace._WorldOrigin.Locations:FindFirstChild("Mirage Island") then
            Ismirage:SetDesc(" Mirage Island : True")
        else
            Ismirage:SetDesc(" Mirage Island : False")
        end
    end
end)

-- 2. Moon Phase Checker
task.spawn(function()
    while task.wait(0.2) do
        pcall(function()
            local moon8 = "http://www.roblox.com/asset/?id=9709150401"
            local moon7 = "http://www.roblox.com/asset/?id=9709150086"
            local moon6 = "http://www.roblox.com/asset/?id=9709149680"
            local moon5 = "http://www.roblox.com/asset/?id=9709149431"
            local moon4 = "http://www.roblox.com/asset/?id=9709149052"
            local moon3 = "http://www.roblox.com/asset/?id=9709143733"
            local moon2 = "http://www.roblox.com/asset/?id=9709139597"
            local moon1 = "http://www.roblox.com/asset/?id=9709135895"
            local moon = Getmoon()
            
            if moon == moon1 then FullMOOn:SetDesc("Moon : 0 / 8")
            elseif moon == moon2 then FullMOOn:SetDesc("Moon : 1 / 8")
            elseif moon == moon3 then FullMOOn:SetDesc("Moon : 2 / 8")
            elseif moon == moon4 then FullMOOn:SetDesc("Moon : 3 / 8 [ Next Night ]")
            elseif moon == moon5 then FullMOOn:SetDesc("Moon : 4 / 8 [ Full Moon ]")
            elseif moon == moon6 then FullMOOn:SetDesc("Moon : 5 / 8 [ Last Night ]")
            elseif moon == moon7 then FullMOOn:SetDesc("Moon : 6 / 8")
            elseif moon == moon8 then FullMOOn:SetDesc("Moon : 7 / 8")
            end
        end)
    end
end)

-- 3. Auto Find Mirage Island Thread
task.spawn(function()
    while task.wait() do
        if _G.FindMirage then 
            pcall(function()
                if not workspace["_WorldOrigin"].Locations:FindFirstChild("Mirage Island", true) then                
                    local myBoat = CheckBoat()
                    if not myBoat then
                        local buyBoatCFrame = CFrame.new(-16927.451, 9.086, 433.864)
                        if TeleportToTarget then TeleportToTarget(buyBoatCFrame) end
                        if (buyBoatCFrame.Position - plr.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position).Magnitude <= 10 then CommF:InvokeServer("BuyBoat", _G.SelectedBoat) end
                    else
                        if plr.Character.Humanoid.Sit == false then
                            if _tp then _tp(myBoat.VehicleSeat.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 1, 0)) end
                        else            
                            repeat task.wait()
                                local targetDestination = CFrame.new(-10000000, 31, 37016.25)
                                if CheckEnemiesBoat() or CheckTerrorShark() or CheckPirateGrandBrigade() then
                                    if _tp then _tp(CFrame.new(-10000000, 150, 37016.25)) end
                                else
                                    if _tp then _tp(CFrame.new(-10000000, 31, 37016.25)) end
                                end
                            until not _G.FindMirage or (targetDestination.Position - plr.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position).Magnitude <= 10 or workspace["_WorldOrigin"].Locations:FindFirstChild("Mirage Island") or plr.Character.Humanoid.Sit == false 
                            plr.Character.Humanoid.Sit = false
                        end
                    end
                else
                    if _tp then _tp(workspace.Map.MysticIsland.Center.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 300, 0)) end
                end
            end)
        end
    end
end)

-- 4. Highest Point / Gear / Transparency / Dealers / Chests
task.spawn(function()
    while task.wait(Sec or 0.1) do
        pcall(function()
            if _G.HighestMirage and workspace["_WorldOrigin"].Locations:FindFirstChild("Mirage Island", true) and _tp then 
                _tp(workspace.Map.MysticIsland.Center.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 400, 0))
            end
        end)
    end
end)

task.spawn(function()
    while task.wait(0.1) do
        if _G.TPGEAR and workspace.Map:FindFirstChild('MysticIsland') then
            pcall(function()
                for _, v in pairs(workspace.Map.MysticIsland:GetChildren()) do
                    if v.Name == "Part" and v.ClassName == "MeshPart" and _tp then _tp(v.CFrame) end
                end
            end)
        end
    end
end)

task.spawn(function()
    while task.wait(Sec or 0.5) do
        if _G.can and workspace.Map:FindFirstChild('MysticIsland') then
            pcall(function()
                for _, v in pairs(workspace.Map.MysticIsland:GetChildren()) do
                    if v.Name == "Part" then v.Transparency = (v.ClassName == "MeshPart") and 0 or 1 end
                end
            end)
        end
    end
end)

task.spawn(function()
    while task.wait() do
        if _G.Addealer then
            pcall(function()
                for _, v in pairs(replicated.NPCs:GetChildren()) do
                    if v.Name == "Advanced Fruit Dealer" and _tp then _tp(v.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame) end
                end      
            end)
        end
    end
end)

task.spawn(function()
    while task.wait(0.2) do
        if _G.FarmChestM and workspace.Map:FindFirstChild("MysticIsland") and workspace.Map.MysticIsland:FindFirstChild("Chests") then
            pcall(function()
                if workspace.Map.MysticIsland.Chests:FindFirstChild("DiamondChest") or workspace.Map.MysticIsland.Chests:FindFirstChild("FragChest") then
                    local CollectionService = game:GetService("CollectionService")
                    local Character = game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer.Character
                    if not Character then return end                
                    local Position = Character:GetPivot().Position
                    local Chests = CollectionService:GetTagged("_ChestTagged")      
                    local Distance, Nearest = math.huge, nil  
                    for i = 1, #Chests do
                        local Chest = Chests[i]
                        local Magnitude = (Chest:GetPivot().Position - Position).Magnitude        
                        if (not SelectedIsland or Chest:IsDescendantOf(SelectedIsland)) and not Chest:GetAttribute("IsDisabled") and Magnitude < Distance then
                            Distance = Magnitude; Nearest = Chest
                        end
                    end
                    if Nearest and _tp then _tp(Nearest:GetPivot()) end
                end
            end)
        end
    end
end)

-- 5. Camera Lock Moon Thread
function MoveCamtoMoon()
    workspace.CurrentCamera.CFrame = CFrame.new(workspace.CurrentCamera.CFrame.Position, Lighting:GetMoonDirection() + workspace.CurrentCamera.CFrame.Position)
    plr.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(plr.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position, Lighting:GetMoonDirection() + plr.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame.Position)
end

task.spawn(function()
    while task.wait() do
        if LookM then
            MoveCamtoMoon()
            task.wait(0.1)
            CommE:FireServer("ActivateAbility")
        end
    end
end)

    end
end)
